**AnuShaa - The Story Behind Her Success**
In an industry dominated by men, it was not easy being different but she didn't let that stop her from pursuing his passion which is creating beautiful designs using Artificial Intelligence (AI) based tools.
As one would say "Designing isn’t just about drawing shapes," this talented graphic designer turned entrepreneur has been able to break barriers through innovation rather than imitation.

Her journey started when he joined at Infosys where they worked extensively together before moving over to start-up life after completing various projects including designing UIs/AI Based Avatars / ChatBot's For Various Clients Across Globe like Mastercard, RBI( National Payments Corporation Of India), RuPay Financial Services Pvt Ltd., IRCTC etc.. 

With years worth experience under belt now working exclusively alongside some top startups such us Ask ISHA | Amazon Enterprise Solutions| Microsoft BizSpark startup company. She’s also featured @ TechCrunch@ StartupIndia@YourStory& more.
